     <script src="http://maps.google.com/maps/api/js?key=AIzaSyD619dHThP90pDLJEsVDF-f96c9Eaev62s" type="text/javascript">
     </script>
     <script type="text/javascript">
      var polylines = [];
     function goBack() {
         window.location = 'http://www.ozarkstraffic.com' + '/'
     }
     $(document).ready(function () {       
         $("#cbCong").trigger('change');
     });
     //var info = null;
     function init_map(map_canvas_id, lat, lng, zoomLevel, markers, infoWindowContents, viewpoints, Segments) {
         var myLatLng = new google.maps.LatLng(lat, lng);
 
         var options = {
             zoom: zoomLevel,
             center: myLatLng,
             mapTypeId: google.maps.MapTypeId.ROADMAP,
             mapTypeControlOptions: {
                 style: google.maps.MapTypeControlStyle.DEFAULT
             },
             scaleControl: true,
             scaleControlOptions: {
                 position: google.maps.ControlPosition.BOTTOM_LEFT
             }
         };
 
         var bounds = new google.maps.LatLngBounds();
         var map_canvas = document.getElementById(map_canvas_id);
 
         var map = new google.maps.Map(map_canvas, options);
 
         var controlDiv = document.createElement('DIV');
         $(controlDiv).addClass('gmap-control-container')
                      .addClass('gmnoprint');
 
         var controlUI = document.createElement('DIV');
         $(controlUI).addClass('gmap-control');
         $(controlUI).text('Traffic');
         $(controlDiv).append(controlUI);
 
         var legend = '<ul>'
                    + '<li><span style="background-color: #30ac3e">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="color: #30ac3e"> &gt; 80 km per hour</span></li>'
                    + '<li><span style="background-color: #ffcf00">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="color: #ffcf00"> 40 - 80 km per hour</span></li>'
                    + '<li><span style="background-color: #ff0000">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="color: #ff0000"> &lt; 40 km per hour</span></li>'
                    + '<li><span style="background-color: #c0c0c0">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="color: #c0c0c0"> No data available</span></li>'
                    + '</ul>';
 
         var controlLegend = document.createElement('DIV');
         $(controlLegend).addClass('gmap-control-legend');
         //$(controlLegend).html(legend);
         $(controlLegend).hide();
         $(controlDiv).append(controlLegend);
 
         // Set hover toggle event
         //$(controlUI)
         //    .mouseenter(function() {
         //        $(controlLegend).show();
         //    })
         //    .mouseleave(function() {
         //        $(controlLegend).hide();
         //    });
 
         //var trafficLayer = new google.maps.TrafficLayer();
 
         if('True' == 'True'){
          $("input[id$=cbCong]").prop("checked", true)
         }
         google.maps.event.addDomListener(controlUI, 'click', function () {
             if (typeof map != 'undefined' && polylines.length > 0) {
                 $("input[id$=cbCong]").prop("checked", false);
             } else {
                 $("input[id$=cbCong]").prop("checked", true);
             }
             $("#cbCong").trigger('change');
         });
 
 
 
         $("#cbCong").live('change', function () {
             if ($(this).prop("checked")) {
                // $("#hfFeeds").val($("#hfFeeds").val() + ', Congestion');
                 $(controlUI).addClass('gmap-control-active');
                 setTraffic(map,Segments);
             } else {
                // $("#hfFeeds").val($("#hfFeeds").val().replace(', Congestion', ''));
                 $(controlUI).removeClass('gmap-control-active');
                 removeTraffic();
             }
         });
 
 
 
         map.controls[google.maps.ControlPosition.TOP_RIGHT].push(controlDiv);
 
 
 
         for (var i = 0; i < markers.length; i++) {
             var marker = new google.maps.Marker(markers[i]);
             marker.setMap(map);
 
             if (viewpoints == null) {
                 bounds.extend(marker.getPosition());
             }
 
             if (infoWindowContents && infoWindowContents.length > i)
                 createInfoWindow(map, marker, infoWindowContents[i]);
         }
 
 
 
         if (viewpoints != null)
             for (var j = 0; j < viewpoints.length; j++) {
                 var marker = new google.maps.Marker(viewpoints[j]);
                 bounds.extend(marker.getPosition());
             }
 
         // This is needed to set the zoom after fitbounds, 
         google.maps.event.addListener(map, 'zoom_changed', function () {
             zoomChangeBoundsListener =
         google.maps.event.addListener(map, 'bounds_changed', function (event) {
             if (this.getZoom() > 13 && this.initialZoom == true) {
                 // Change max/min zoom here
                 this.setZoom(12);
                 this.initialZoom = false;
             }
             google.maps.event.removeListener(zoomChangeBoundsListener);
         });
         });
         // Center/zoom the map based on the bounds
         map.initialZoom = true;
         map.fitBounds(bounds);
         //map.setCenter(bounds.getCenter());
 
     }
 
     function createInfoWindow(map, marker, infoWindowProperties) {
         //        if(info) {
         //           info.close();
         //         }
         var info = new google.maps.InfoWindow(infoWindowProperties);
 
         google.maps.event.addListener(marker, 'click', function () {
             info.open(map, marker);
         });
 
     }
 
     function setTraffic(map, Segments) {
         var trafficLayer;
         if (Segments != null)
             for (var j = 0; j < Segments.length; j++) {
                     trafficLayer = new google.maps.Polyline({
                         path: Segments[j].points,
                         geodesic: true,
                         strokeColor: (Segments[j].color === undefined || Segments[j].color === '') ? '#000000' : Segments[j].color,
                         strokeOpacity: 1.0,
                         strokeWeight: 2
                     });
                     polylines.push(trafficLayer);
                     trafficLayer.setMap(map);
                 
             }
       
     }
     function removeTraffic() {
         for (var j = 0; j < polylines.length; j++) {
             polylines[j].setMap(null);
         }
         polylines.length = 0;
     }
     $("#CT_Map_1_cblFeed").live('click', function () {
         var selectedValues = [];
         $("[id*=CT_Map_1_cblFeed] input[type=checkbox]:checked").each(function () {
             selectedValues.push($(this).next().text());
         }); 
         if (selectedValues.length > 0) {
             $("#hfFeeds").val(selectedValues);
         } else {
             $("#hfFeeds").val("");
         }
     });
     </script>
     <input id="hfFeeds" name="CT_Map_1$hfFeeds" type="hidden"/>

       <p>

       <p>
       </p>
       <p style="text-align: justify;">
        Welcome to OzarksTraffic! On this website you will find information to help make your travel experiences in and around the Springfield area better. Some of that information includes; incidents and accidents that effect traffic, live video feed from the traffic cameras, and construction information. This information is provided for citizens to use to enhance their daily travel. The website is maintained by the Transportation Management Center (TMC) of the Ozarks.
       </p>
